\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\subsubsection*{template$<$ui dim$>$\newline
struct mpmd$<$ dim $>$}

This structure takes care of Monge patch molecular dynamics simulations. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_source_l00617}{617}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_source}{libmd.\+h}}.

bool \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::add\+\_\+bond (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{interaction }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Add a bond. 

This function adds a bond between particles {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} of previously-\/defined interaction type {\ttfamily interaction}. (See the \mbox{\hyperlink{md_doc_markdown_interactions_md-pairpotentials}{Interactions}} documentation for more information on interaction types.) ~\newline
~\newline
 Does nothing and returns false if one of the following holds\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item an interaction already exists between {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2}, 
\item the interaction specified by the third argument does not exist or was previously removed. 
\end{DoxyItemize}Otherwise, creates a bond of the specified type between {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2}, and returns {\ttfamily true}.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{bonds_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00042}{42}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{bonds_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{bonds.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

bool \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::add\+\_\+bond (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{potential,  }\item[{std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}} $>$ \&}]{parameters }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Add a bond. 

This function adds a bond between particles {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} with the potential type and parameters specified in the arguments. (See the \mbox{\hyperlink{md_doc_markdown_interactions_md-pairpotentials}{Interactions}} documentation for more information on potential types and passing parameters.) ~\newline
~\newline
 Does nothing if an interaction already exists between {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2}, and returns {\ttfamily false}. Otherwise, creates a bond of the specified type between {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2}, and returns {\ttfamily true}.

Add a particle to the system. 

This function adds a particle to the system and returns its index. Optionally, provide its mass (default\+: 1.\+0), type (default\+: 0) and/or whether it is fixed (default\+: false). The position and velocity of the new particle are not set.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
bool \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::add\+\_\+sp\+\_\+bond (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{interaction }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Add a superparticle bond. 

This function creates a new superparticle type and assigns it to the superparticle that {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} belong to. It then adds an interaction between the two particles, using element {\ttfamily interaction} from {\ttfamily network.\+library\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}. If the two particles are not in the same superparticle, or have an interaction already, it does nothing and returns false.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
bool \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::add\+\_\+sp\+\_\+bond (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{potential,  }\item[{std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}} $>$ \&}]{parameters }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Add a superparticle bond. 

This function creates a new superparticle type and assigns it to the superparticle that {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} belong to. It then adds an interaction between the two particles, using a new interaction of the given type and with the given parameters. If the two particles are not in the same superparticle, or have an interaction already, it does nothing and returns false.

Add superparticle interaction rule. 

This function adds an interaction between particle numbers {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} of superparticles of type {\ttfamily spt}, using element {\ttfamily interaction} from {\ttfamily network.\+library\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}. It returns whether the given superparticletype and interaction exist and the particle numbers do not already have an interaction. If the two particle numbers already have an interaction, it is not modified.

Add superparticle interaction rule. 

This function adds an interaction between particle numbers {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} of superparticles of type {\ttfamily spt}, using a new interaction of the given type and with the given parameters. It returns whether the given superparticletype exists and the particle numbers do not already have an interaction. If the two particle numbers already have an interaction, it is not modified and the interaction is not added to {\ttfamily network.\+library\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}.

bool \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::add\+\_\+typeinteraction (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{type1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{type2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{potential,  }\item[{std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}} $>$ \&}]{parameters }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Add type interaction rule. 

This function adds a type interaction between the given types, using a new interaction of the given type and with the given parameters. It returns whether the two types do not already have an interaction. If the two types already have an interaction, it is not modified and the interaction is not added to {\ttfamily network.\+library\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::bruteforce\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Bruteforce indexing algorithm. 

This brute force indexing algorithm simply checks every pair of particles.~\newline
 This function is to be preferred over \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_af99c7ccc16292d4c1cdb07bd0c9ac895_af99c7ccc16292d4c1cdb07bd0c9ac895}{md$<$dim$>$\+::cell()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_a7a10193ac507980720263dd95d259958_a7a10193ac507980720263dd95d259958}{md$<$dim$>$\+::kdtree()}} if all (or most) particles are within {\ttfamily network.\+ssz} of each other.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00369}{369}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{index.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

\index{mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}!cell@{cell}}
\index{cell@{cell}!mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cell()}{cell()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::cell\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Cell indexing algorithm. 

This indexing algorithm uses the cell method.~\newline
 The system is divided into cells of equal size, which are at least {\ttfamily network.\+ssz} in size in each dimension. The particles are put in their corresponding cells. Two particles that are in cells that do not share at least a corner will be more than {\ttfamily network.\+ssz} apart, therefore such pairs of cells need not be checked.~\newline


Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00265}{265}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{index.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{clear()}{clear()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::clear\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Clear all particles and interactions. 

Remove all particles from the \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}} structure, and clear all data types storing interactions and superparticle data. Leaves the system box and the boundary conditions unchanged.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00050}{50}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{md_8libmd_8cc_source}{md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{clone\_particle()}{clone\_particle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::clone\+\_\+particle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{i,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}}}]{x\mbox{[}dim\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Clone a particle and translate. 

This function creates a new particle that is a copy of particle {\ttfamily i}. The position of the new particle is translated by the vector {\ttfamily x\mbox{[}\mbox{]}} with respect to the original one. It returns the index of the new particle.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{structmd_afa87cd3c320aca8244308b650a63b919_afa87cd3c320aca8244308b650a63b919}\label{structmd_afa87cd3c320aca8244308b650a63b919_afa87cd3c320aca8244308b650a63b919}} 
\index{mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}!clone\_sp@{clone\_sp}}
\index{clone\_sp@{clone\_sp}!mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{clone\_sp()}{clone\_sp()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::clone\+\_\+sp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{spi,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}}}]{x\mbox{[}dim\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Clone a superparticle and translate. 

This function creates a new superparticle that is a copy of the superparticle with index {\ttfamily spi}, with new particles. The position of all the new particles are translated by the vector {\ttfamily x\mbox{[}\mbox{]}} with respect to the original ones. It returns the index of the new superparticle in {\ttfamily network.\+superparticles\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{sp_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00198}{198}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{sp_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{sp.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{structmd_a3e91b0575628071b6a0175f2b40b0c93_a3e91b0575628071b6a0175f2b40b0c93}\label{structmd_a3e91b0575628071b6a0175f2b40b0c93_a3e91b0575628071b6a0175f2b40b0c93}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{clone\_sptype()}{clone\_sptype()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::clone\+\_\+sptype (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{sp }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Make a new sptype for superparticle sp if it is not unique to sp. 

This function creates a new superparticle type that is exactly the same as that of superparticle {\ttfamily spi}, assigns it to the superparticle and returns its index in {\ttfamily network.\+sptypes\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}. If superparticle {\ttfamily spi} is the only superparticle of its type, this fuction does nothing and returns the index of its type in {\ttfamily network.\+sptypes\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{bonds_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00382}{382}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{bonds_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{bonds.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

References \mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_source_l00056}{U\+I\+\_\+\+M\+AX}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{structmd_af4b990db21034be32837761098e03336_af4b990db21034be32837761098e03336}\label{structmd_af4b990db21034be32837761098e03336_af4b990db21034be32837761098e03336}} 
\index{mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}!dap@{dap}}
\index{dap@{dap}!mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{dap()}{dap()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::dap (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{d,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}}}]{ad }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Manipulate particle distances with respect to periodic boundary conditions. 

Given a displacement {\ttfamily ad} and corresponding spatial dimension {\ttfamily d}, calculates the displacement modulo the periodic box size in that dimension.

Under periodic boundary conditions, distances are required to lie in the range {\ttfamily (-\/simbox.\+L\mbox{[}d\mbox{]}/2,simbox.\+L\mbox{[}d\mbox{]}/2)}. If the displacement {\ttfamily dap} is outside this range, multiples of {\ttfamily simbox.\+L\mbox{[}d\mbox{]}} are added or subtracted until the displacement is within these bounds, and the result is returned.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{distances_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00006}{6}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{distances_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{distances.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

Calculate difference in particle positions in certain dimension i by particle index. 

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

This version accepts as inputs the coordinates of two points in arrays {\ttfamily x1\mbox{[}dim\mbox{]}} and {\ttfamily x2\mbox{[}dim\mbox{]}} and returns the (periodic) distance between them along spatial dimension {\ttfamily d}.

Calculate difference in particle positions in certain dimension i by particle index. 

Returns the distance between points indexed by {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} along spatial dimension {\ttfamily d}. If periodic boundary conditions are used, the distance is between the closest periodic images of the two points.

Calculate distances between two particles (squared) ldf \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_aa8d0c1ecf0b5cd3acfda235bf4d7939c_aa8d0c1ecf0b5cd3acfda235bf4d7939c}{distsq(ui p1,ldf x2\mbox{[}dim\mbox{]})}}; ///$<$ Calculate distances between two particles (squared) 

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

This version accepts as inputs the coordinates of two points in arrays {\ttfamily x1\mbox{[}dim\mbox{]}} and {\ttfamily x2\mbox{[}dim\mbox{]}} and returns the squared (periodic) distance between them.

Calculate distances between two particles (squared) 

Returns the square of the distance between points indexed by {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2}. If periodic boundary conditions are used, the distance is between the closest periodic images of the two points.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{structmd_a6d7f9c3ed6d212f1b34b2d2e94b7fd33_a6d7f9c3ed6d212f1b34b2d2e94b7fd33}\label{structmd_a6d7f9c3ed6d212f1b34b2d2e94b7fd33_a6d7f9c3ed6d212f1b34b2d2e94b7fd33}} 
\index{mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}!dv@{dv}}
\index{dv@{dv}!mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{dv()}{dv()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::dv (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{d,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Calculate difference in particle velocities in certain dimension i by particle index. 

Returns the {\ttfamily d}th component of the velocity difference between the closest periodic image of two particles indexed by {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2}. If the vector connecting the periodic images crosses a sheared boundary, the resulting velocity difference takes into account the shear velocity of the periodic image as well. The result is returned as a $d$-\/dimensional array of velocity components.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{distances_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00137}{137}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{distances_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{distances.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

Save forces from arrays. 

This function takes an arbitrary number of arrays. ~\newline
 The array is assumed to be of length N, the number of particles. ~\newline
 Then for each {\ttfamily i}th particle force every {\ttfamily d}th component is assigned to that array ~\newline
 As {\ttfamily d} is a variadic variable it is stored and increased for every array. This function checks if forces need to be recalculated

This function takes an arbitrary number of values. ~\newline
 Then for each {\ttfamily i}th particle position every {\ttfamily d}th component is assigned to that value ~\newline
 As {\ttfamily d} is a variadic variable it is stored and increased for every array.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{structmd_a50bf4ccf11941a53886388e01580d55f_a50bf4ccf11941a53886388e01580d55f}\label{structmd_a50bf4ccf11941a53886388e01580d55f_a50bf4ccf11941a53886388e01580d55f}} 
\index{mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}!import\_force@{import\_force}}
\index{import\_force@{import\_force}!mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{import\_force()}{import\_force()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::import\+\_\+force (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}} $\ast$}]{F }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Load forces from arrays. 

This function takes an arbitrary number of arrays. ~\newline
 The array is assumed to be of length N, the number of particles. ~\newline
 Each {\ttfamily i}th element is then assigned to the particle the {\ttfamily d}th component of the particle\textquotesingle{}s force~\newline
 As {\ttfamily d} is a variadic variable it is stored and increased for every array.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{importexport_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00102}{102}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{importexport_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{importexport.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

template$<$typename... arg$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::import\+\_\+force (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}} $\ast$}]{F,  }\item[{arg...}]{argv }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Load forces from arrays. 

This function takes an arbitrary number of arrays. ~\newline
 The array is assumed to be of length N, the number of particles. ~\newline
 Each {\ttfamily i}th element is then assigned to the particle the {\ttfamily d}th component of the particle\textquotesingle{}s force~\newline
 As {\ttfamily d} is a variadic variable it is stored and increased for every array.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{importexport_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00114}{114}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{importexport_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{importexport.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::import\+\_\+vel (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{i,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}}}]{dx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Load velocity for i from value. 

This function takes an arbitrary number of values. ~\newline
 The values are then then assigned to the {\ttfamily d}th component of the {\ttfamily i}th particle\textquotesingle{}s velocity ~\newline
 As {\ttfamily d} is a variadic variable it is stored and increased for every value.

\index{mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}!index@{index}}
\index{index@{index}!mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{index()}{index()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::index\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Find neighbors. 

This function finds all the pairs of particles that are within {\ttfamily network.\+ssz} of each other and have an interaction. They are then put in each other\textquotesingle{}s skinlist ({\ttfamily network.\+skins\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}).~\newline
 It calls the algorithm specificied by {\ttfamily indexdata.\+method}\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_a32c3d5e5fe53203d0754ac9706bd0f21_a32c3d5e5fe53203d0754ac9706bd0f21}{md$<$dim$>$\+::bruteforce()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_a7a10193ac507980720263dd95d259958_a7a10193ac507980720263dd95d259958}{md$<$dim$>$\+::kdtree()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_af99c7ccc16292d4c1cdb07bd0c9ac895_af99c7ccc16292d4c1cdb07bd0c9ac895}{md$<$dim$>$\+::cell()}}.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00014}{14}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{index.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

\index{mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}!integrate@{integrate}}
\index{integrate@{integrate}!mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{integrate()}{integrate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmpmd}{mpmd}}$<$ dim $>$\+::integrate\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [final]}, {\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Integrate particle trajectoriess. 

This function is the Monge patch analog to \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_a7254ea0201ee881fd53c6722e6473e5f_a7254ea0201ee881fd53c6722e6473e5f}{md$<$dim$>$\+::integrate()}} and calculates the particle trajectories. ~\newline
 After integrating (and updating the particle) it call \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_a0395ea5f8b917457f3775b59da0b3734_a0395ea5f8b917457f3775b59da0b3734}{md$<$dim$>$\+::periodicity()}}, and calculates the geomatric derivatives for the new particle position.

Reimplemented from \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_a7254ea0201ee881fd53c6722e6473e5f_a7254ea0201ee881fd53c6722e6473e5f}{md$<$ dim $>$}}.



Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{mpmd_8libmd_8cc_source_l00228}{228}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{mpmd_8libmd_8cc_source}{mpmd.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

Dump interactions of a certain particle into a table. 

This function puts a list of all interaction neighbors of particle {\ttfamily i} in {\ttfamily table}, as pairs of particles with {\ttfamily i} being the first.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{kdtree()}{kdtree()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::kdtree\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



k-\/d tree indexing algorithm 

This indexing function uses a k-\/d tree (a multidimensional binary tree).~\newline
 It makes use of the recursive functions \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_a8ab281a337c8448f30b808ef51be99e6_a8ab281a337c8448f30b808ef51be99e6}{md$<$dim$>$\+::kdtree\+\_\+build()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_af6fbb4becba7012a1914b5eee637d718_af6fbb4becba7012a1914b5eee637d718}{md$<$dim$>$\+::kdtree\+\_\+index()}}.~\newline
 It does not work if there is both shear and a dimension with periodic boundary conditions.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00140}{140}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{index.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

References \mbox{\hyperlink{enums_8libmd_8h_source_l00007}{B\+C\+O\+N\+D\+::\+B\+O\+X\+S\+H\+E\+AR}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{macros_8libmd_8h_source_l00058}{E\+R\+R\+OR}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{enums_8libmd_8h_source_l00007}{B\+C\+O\+N\+D\+::\+P\+E\+R\+I\+O\+D\+IC}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{structmd_a8ab281a337c8448f30b808ef51be99e6_a8ab281a337c8448f30b808ef51be99e6}\label{structmd_a8ab281a337c8448f30b808ef51be99e6_a8ab281a337c8448f30b808ef51be99e6}} 
\index{mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}!kdtree\_build@{kdtree\_build}}
\index{kdtree\_build@{kdtree\_build}!mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{kdtree\_build()}{kdtree\_build()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::kdtree\+\_\+build (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{first,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{last,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



k-\/d tree indexing algorithm\+: tree build function (recursive) 

This function recursively builds the k-\/d tree, to be used by \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_a7a10193ac507980720263dd95d259958_a7a10193ac507980720263dd95d259958}{md$<$dim$>$\+::kdtree()}}.~\newline
 The particles in the subtree marked by {\ttfamily first} and {\ttfamily last} at recursion depth {\ttfamily level} are split into two subtrees of (about) equal size. The particles in one subtree have a lower value of their position coordinate in a given dimension than the particles in the other subtree. The dimension is specified by {\ttfamily indexdata.\+kdtreedata.\+Divide\+By\+Dim\mbox{[}level\mbox{]}}, which is set by \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_a7a10193ac507980720263dd95d259958_a7a10193ac507980720263dd95d259958}{md$<$dim$>$\+::kdtree()}}. The two subtrees are build recursively.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00060}{60}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{index.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061 \{   }
\DoxyCodeLine{00062     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (last -\/ first == 1) \textcolor{comment}{// Leaf}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070     \{   \textcolor{comment}{// Set minimum and maximum value equal to the position of this particle (Idx[first])}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{kdtree\_index()}{kdtree\_index()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::kdtree\+\_\+index (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{first1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{last1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{first2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{last2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



k-\/d tree indexing algorithm\+: neighbor finder (recursive) 

This function recursively finds neighboring particles, one from subtree 1, the other from subtree 2 (possibly the same subtree).~\newline
 First it is checked if the subtrees are too far apart; nothing is done then. Otherwise, the function is called for every combination of subtrees. When a leaf is reached, the single particle is checked against the particle{\bfseries{}}(s) in the other subtree.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00091}{91}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{index.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::mad\+\_\+bond (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{interaction }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Force add/modify bond. 

Same as \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_a21674b3d7fe619e81706e844e47bd564_a21674b3d7fe619e81706e844e47bd564}{md$<$dim$>$\+::add\+\_\+bond(ui p1, ui p2, ui interaction)}}, but performs no checks. ~\newline
~\newline
 {\bfseries{Warning\+:}} Assumes that the specified interaction type actually exists, and replaces any previously defined interaction between {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::mad\+\_\+sp\+\_\+bond (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{interaction }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Force add/modify superparticle bond. 

This function creates a new superparticle type and assigns it to the superparticle that {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} belong to. It then assigns an interaction to the two particles, using element {\ttfamily interaction} from {\ttfamily network.\+library\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}. It does not perform any checks.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::mad\+\_\+sp\+\_\+bond (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{potential,  }\item[{std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}} $>$ \&}]{parameters }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Force add/modify superparticle bond. 

This function creates a new superparticle type and assigns it to the superparticle that {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} belong to. It then assigns an interaction to the two particles, using a new interaction of the given type and with the given parameters. It does not perform any checks.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mad\_sp\_interaction()}{mad\_sp\_interaction()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::mad\+\_\+sp\+\_\+interaction (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{spt,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{interaction }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Force add/mod superparticle interaction rule. 

This function assigns an interaction to particle numbers {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} of superparticles of type {\ttfamily spt}, using element {\ttfamily interaction} from {\ttfamily network.\+library\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}. If the given superparticletype does not exist, a new one is added to {\ttfamily network.\+sptypes\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}. It returns the index of the superparticletype (which is {\ttfamily spt} or the index of the newly created one). It does not perform any checks.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::mad\+\_\+sp\+\_\+interaction (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{spt,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{potential,  }\item[{std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}} $>$ \&}]{parameters }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Force add/mod superparticle interaction rule. 

This function assigns an interaction to particle numbers {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} of superparticles of type {\ttfamily spt}, using a new interaction of the given type and with the given parameters. If the given superparticletype does not exist, a new one is added to {\ttfamily network.\+sptypes\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}. It returns the index of the superparticletype (which is {\ttfamily spt} or the index of the newly created one). It does not perform any checks.

bool \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::mod\+\_\+bond (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{interaction }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Modify a bond. 

This function modifies any previous interaction between particles {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2}, and turns it into a bond of previously-\/defined interaction type specified in the third argument. (See the \mbox{\hyperlink{md_doc_markdown_interactions_md-pairpotentials}{Interactions}} documentation for more information on interaction types.) ~\newline
~\newline
 Does nothing and returns false if one of the following holds\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item no interaction exists between {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2}, 
\item the interaction specified by the third argument does not exist or was previously removed. 
\end{DoxyItemize}Otherwise, creates a bond of the specified type between {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2}, and returns {\ttfamily true}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
bool \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::mod\+\_\+sp\+\_\+bond (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{interaction }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Modify a superparticle bond. 

This function creates a new superparticle type and assigns it to the superparticle that {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} belong to. It then modifies the interaction between the two particles, using element {\ttfamily interaction} from {\ttfamily network.\+library\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}. If the two particles are not in the same superparticle, or do not have an interaction already, it does nothing and returns false.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
bool \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::mod\+\_\+sp\+\_\+bond (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{potential,  }\item[{std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}} $>$ \&}]{parameters }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Modify a superparticle bond. 

This function creates a new superparticle type and assigns it to the superparticle that {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} belong to. It then modifies the interaction between the two particles, using a new interaction of the given type and with the given parameters. If the two particles are not in the same superparticle, or do not have an interaction already, it does nothing and returns false.

Modify superparticle interaction rule. 

This function modifies the interaction between particle numbers {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} of superparticles of type {\ttfamily spt}, using element {\ttfamily interaction} from {\ttfamily network.\+library\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}. It returns whether the given superparticletype and interaction exist and the particle numbers already had an interaction. If the two particle numbers do not already have an interaction, it is not added.

Modify superparticle interaction rule. 

This function modifies the interaction between particle numbers {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} of superparticles of type {\ttfamily spt}, using a new interaction of the given type and with the given parameters. It returns whether the given superparticletype and interaction exist and the particle numbers already had an interaction. If the two particle numbers do not already have an interaction, it is not added and the interaction is not added to {\ttfamily network.\+library\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}.

Modify type interaction rule. 

This function modifies the type interaction between the given types, using a new interaction of the given type and with the given parameters. It returns whether the two types already had an interaction. If the two types do not already have an interaction, it is not added and the interaction is not added to {\ttfamily network.\+library\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}.

\index{mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}!periodicity@{periodicity}}
\index{periodicity@{periodicity}!mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{periodicity()}{periodicity()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::periodicity\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Called after integration to keep the particle within the defined boundaries. 

Update positions and velocities of particles to respect the appropriate boundary conditions. ~\newline
 This function loops through the {\ttfamily dim} dimensions, and updates the positions and velocities of all (non-\/fixed) particles that have passed through the boundary perpendicular to dimension {\ttfamily d}, based on the value of {\ttfamily simbox.\+bcond\mbox{[}d\mbox{]}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{structmd_a8f9f008ef44668edcc81465ee6fc633d_a8f9f008ef44668edcc81465ee6fc633d}\label{structmd_a8f9f008ef44668edcc81465ee6fc633d_a8f9f008ef44668edcc81465ee6fc633d}} 
\index{mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}!rem\_particle@{rem\_particle}}
\index{rem\_particle@{rem\_particle}!mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rem\_particle()}{rem\_particle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::rem\+\_\+particle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{i }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Remove a particle from the system. 

This function removes particle {\ttfamily i} and all references to it from the system.~\newline
 Note\+: particle {\ttfamily N-\/1} becomes the new particle {\ttfamily i} (if $i<N-1$).

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{particles_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00076}{76}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{particles_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{particles.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
bool \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::rem\+\_\+sp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{spi }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Remove a superparticle (i.\+e. the structure, not the particles) 

This function removes the superparticle with index {\ttfamily spi} from {\ttfamily network.\+superparticles\mbox{[}\mbox{]}} and resets the superparticle reference ({\ttfamily network.\+spid\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}) of all its particles. It returns whether the given superparticle existed.~\newline
 Note\+: the last superparticle in {\ttfamily network.\+superparticles\mbox{[}\mbox{]}} takes the place of the removed one

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{sp_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00018}{18}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{sp_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{sp.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rem\_sp\_bond()}{rem\_sp\_bond()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
bool \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::rem\+\_\+sp\+\_\+bond (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Remove a superparticle bond from the system. 

This function creates a new superparticle type and assigns it to the superparticle that {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} belong to. It then removes the interaction between the two particles. If the two particles are not in the same superparticle, or do not have an interaction, it does nothing and returns false.

Delete superparticle interaction rule. 

This function removes the interaction between particle numbers {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2} of superparticles of type {\ttfamily spt}. It does not remove the interaction from{\ttfamily network.\+library\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}. It returns whether the given superparticletype exists and the two particle numbers had an interaction.

Remove all particles in a superparticle. 

This function removes all the particles of the superparticle with index {\ttfamily spi} from the system and clears the superparticle (but does not remove it). It returns whether the given superparticle exists.

Enables Langevin thermostat (and damping) and sets T and gamma (does not use metric) 

This function adds a Langevin thermostat with the given coefficient T and gamma, or changes the coefficient if it was already set.

void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::set\+\_\+reserve (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}}}]{ssz,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{M }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Set reserve memory according to skin size and some arbitrary number of particles. 

This function reserves space for the vectors in {\ttfamily network.\+skins\mbox{[}\mbox{]}}, the amount of space being based on the assumption that each particle has at most {\ttfamily M} particles it interacts with and they are uniformly distributed over the system.

void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::skinner (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{i,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{j,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}}}]{sszsq }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Places interactionneighbor in skin. 

This function is used by the indexing algorithms. It checks if the squared distance between particles {\ttfamily i} and {\ttfamily j} is less than {\ttfamily sszsq} and if they have a (superparticle) type interaction; if so, it adds them (with the interaction) to each other\textquotesingle{}s skinlist.~\newline

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sp\_dispose\_idx()}{sp\_dispose\_idx()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
bool \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::sp\+\_\+dispose\+\_\+idx (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{spi,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{idx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Remove a particle from a superparticle. 

This function removes the particle from slot {\ttfamily idx} of the superparticle with index {\ttfamily spi} from the superparticle (but not from the system). It returns whether the given superparticle exists and has a particle in the given slot.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{sp_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00135}{135}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{sp_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{sp.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{structmd_a1857afeac7bf05251c88d72840f696cd_a1857afeac7bf05251c88d72840f696cd}\label{structmd_a1857afeac7bf05251c88d72840f696cd_a1857afeac7bf05251c88d72840f696cd}}

\index{sp\_ingest@{sp\_ingest}!mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sp\_ingest()}{sp\_ingest()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::sp\+\_\+ingest (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{spi,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{i,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{idx = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a027c70e4468b8d7fb673dec474df6902_a027c70e4468b8d7fb673dec474df6902}{U\+I\+\_\+\+M\+AX}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Add a particle to a superparticle. 

This function puts particle {\ttfamily i} in slot {\ttfamily idx} of the superparticle with index {\ttfamily spi}. If {\ttfamily idx} = {\ttfamily U\+I\+\_\+\+M\+AX}, the index is set to highest index plus one. It returns the index. If the given superparticle does not exist, or the given particle is already in a superparticle, or the given slot is already taken, nothing is done and U\+I\+\_\+\+M\+AX is returned.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{sp_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00071}{71}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{sp_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{sp.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

Reverse lookup of particle id in superparticle. 

This function returns the id of the particle in slot {\ttfamily idx} of the superparticle with index {\ttfamily spi}. If the superparticle does not exist or it does not have a particle in the given slot, it returns U\+I\+\_\+\+M\+AX.

\index{mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}!test\_index@{test\_index}}
\index{test\_index@{test\_index}!mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{test\_index()}{test\_index()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
bool \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::test\+\_\+index\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Test if we need to run the indexing algorithm. 

This function determines if re-\/indexing is necessary, based on the position of each particle at the last time of indexing ({\ttfamily xsk\mbox{[}\mbox{]}})\+: If no particle has moved by more than $(ssz-rco)/2$, then there is no pair of particles that were more than {\ttfamily network.\+ssz} apart, but now less than {\ttfamily network.\+rco} apart, so re-\/indexing is not necessary. Otherwise, re-\/indexing might be necessary and thus should be done.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00037}{37}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{index.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::thread\+\_\+cell (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{c }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Cell indexer for cell c (thread) 

This function finds the neighbors of all particles in cell {\ttfamily c}. It does this by considering (half of) all neighboring cells, such that no pairs of cells are processed twice.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00183}{183}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{index_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{index.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::thread\+\_\+seuler (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{i }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Symplectic euler integrator (threaded) 

This function integrates particle {\ttfamily i} using symplectic Euler. ~\newline
 The symplectic Euler integrator is simpelest (and fastest) symplectic integrator. ~\newline
 The integrator is a first order integrator. ~\newline
 Sometimes symplectic Euler is also refered\+: to as Semi-\/implicit Euler, Euler--Cromer or Newton-\/\+Stoermer-\/\+Verlet. ~\newline
 Symplectic Euler takes the following form\+: \begin{align} \dot{x}^{\mu}_{t+1}=&\dot{x}^{\mu}_{t}+\tfrac{h}{m} F^{\mu}_{t}\\ x^{\mu}_{t+1}=& x^{\mu}_{t}+h\dot{x}^{\mu}_{t+1}\end{align}

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{integrator_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00006}{6}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{integrator_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{integrator.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

Calculate potential energy. 

This function calculates the potential energy of a particle {\ttfamily i} in the presence of curvature.

Reimplemented from \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_a4220b18f9181ca58e4c943ddc204036a_a4220b18f9181ca58e4c943ddc204036a}{md$<$ dim $>$}}.

void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::thread\+\_\+vverlet\+\_\+dx (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{i }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Velocity verlet integrator for velocity (threaded) 

This function integrates particle velocity {\ttfamily i} using Velocity Verlet. ~\newline
 See \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_a151360bcbdea5b086399aded05d7ade8_a151360bcbdea5b086399aded05d7ade8}{md$<$dim$>$\+::thread\+\_\+vverlet\+\_\+x}} for the particle position part. ~\newline
 Velocity Verlet is a second order symplectic integrator. ~\newline
 It is slower than symplectic Euler (see \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_ab268b10a893abd008382df06da416a5a_ab268b10a893abd008382df06da416a5a}{md$<$dim$>$\+::thread\+\_\+seuler}}), yet more accurate. ~\newline
 Velocity Verlet takes the following form\+: \begin{align}x^{\mu}_{t+1}=&x^{\mu}_{t}+h\dot{x}^{\mu}_{t}+\tfrac{h^2}{2}F^{\mu}_{t}\\ \dot{x}^{\mu}_{t+1}=&\dot{x}^{\mu}_{t}+\tfrac{h}{2}(F^{\mu}_{t}+F^{\mu}_{t+1})\end{align} Because of the second force ( $F^{\mu}_{t+1}$) calculation this function is split in two. ~\newline

Velocity verlet integrator for position (threaded) 

This function integrates particle position {\ttfamily i} using Velocity Verlet. ~\newline
 See \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_aab0e1d2ec505cfb5160de37b470c1f1b_aab0e1d2ec505cfb5160de37b470c1f1b}{md$<$dim$>$\+::thread\+\_\+vverlet\+\_\+dx}} for the particle velocity part. ~\newline
 Velocity Verlet is a second order symplectic integrator. ~\newline
 It is slower than symplectic Euler (see \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd_ab268b10a893abd008382df06da416a5a_ab268b10a893abd008382df06da416a5a}{md$<$dim$>$\+::thread\+\_\+seuler}}), yet more accurate. ~\newline
 Velocity Verlet takes the following form\+: \begin{align}x^{\mu}_{t+1}=&x^{\mu}_{t}+h\dot{x}^{\mu}_{t}+\tfrac{h^2}{2}F^{\mu}_{t}\\ \dot{x}^{\mu}_{t+1}=&\dot{x}^{\mu}_{t}+\tfrac{h}{2}(F^{\mu}_{t}+F^{\mu}_{t+1})\end{align} Because of the second force ( $F^{\mu}_{t+1}$) calculation this function is split in two. ~\newline

The van Zuiden integrator for Riemannian manifolds (fails for pseudo-\/\+Riemannian manifolds) 

This function runs the van Zuiden integrator with fixed point iterations and updates the position and velocity for particle {\ttfamily i} accordingly. This function unlike \mbox{\hyperlink{structmpmd_a8e7d1b7cafc905e283023a6b822cc766_a8e7d1b7cafc905e283023a6b822cc766}{mpmd$<$dim$>$\+::thread\+\_\+zuiden\+\_\+protect(ui i)}} waits until the integrator has converged.

void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmpmd}{mpmd}}$<$ dim $>$\+::thread\+\_\+zuiden\+\_\+protect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{i }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



The van Zuiden integrator with protected fixed point itterations (makes sure you don\textquotesingle{}t get stuck in a loop) 

This function runs the van Zuiden integrator with fixed point iterations and updates the position and velocity for particle {\ttfamily i} accordingly. Should the integrator not converge after {\ttfamily integrator.\+generations} iterations this function stops with the fixed point iterations.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{mpmd_8libmd_8cc_source_l00092}{92}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{mpmd_8libmd_8cc_source}{mpmd.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

 If there is a boxshear present it updates the boundaries.

\index{mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}!update\_boundaries@{update\_boundaries}}
\index{update\_boundaries@{update\_boundaries}!mpmd$<$ dim $>$@{mpmd$<$ dim $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{update\_boundaries()}{update\_boundaries()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::update\+\_\+boundaries\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Shifts the periodic boxes appropriately for sheared BC. 

Update the box matrix using the shear velocities. Increments the box matrix $L_{ij}$ (stored in {\ttfamily simbox.\+Lshear}) by $h\times v_{ij}$ where $v_{ij}$ is the shear velocity matrix (stored in {\ttfamily simbox.\+vshear}) and $h$ is the integration timestep (stored in {\ttfamily integrator.\+h}). ~\newline
 Also shifts $L_{ij}$ to ensure that it remains within the bounds $-L_{ii}/2 \leq L_{ij} \leq L_{ii}/2$.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{periodicity_8md_8libmd_8cc_source_l00043}{43}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{periodicity_8md_8libmd_8cc_source}{periodicity.\+md.\+libmd.\+cc}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmd}{md}}$<$ dim $>$\+::update\+\_\+skins (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p1,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{p2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}



Modify skins after adding/modifying/removing bond. 

Updates the skin lists of {\ttfamily p1} and {\ttfamily p2}. This function is called by functions that modify pairwise interactions between specific particle pairs, to rebuild the skins taking into account new particle ID assignments and interaction definitions.

Calculates $g^{\rho \sigma} A_{\sigma \mu \nu} \epsilon^{\mu} \epsilon^{\nu}$ for particle i of the van Zuiden integrator. 

This function calculates $g^{\rho \sigma} A_{\sigma \mu \nu} \epsilon^{\mu} \epsilon^{\nu}$ for particle i of the van Zuiden integrator for particle {\ttfamily i}. It overwrites {\ttfamily ldf eps\mbox{[}dim\mbox{]}} after it is read as input.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$ui dim$>$ \\
void \mbox{\hyperlink{structmpmd}{mpmd}}$<$ dim $>$\+::zuiden\+\_\+C (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7_aa0f39ee33b87675e11229913d432ffe7}{ui}}}]{i,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmd_8h_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea_a9b1cd8bf0a06d4a62c19f7953a3487ea}{ldf}}}]{ZC\mbox{[}dim\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calculates $g^{\rho \sigma} C_{\sigma}$ for particle i of the van Zuiden integrator. 

This function calculates $g^{\rho \sigma} C_{\sigma} = g^{\rho \sigma} (g^p_{\sigma \mu}(x^{\mu}-x^{\mu}_p)+h^2 \frac{F^{\sigma}}{m}) $ for particle i of the van Zuiden integrator for particle {\ttfamily i}. It overwrites {\ttfamily ldf ZC\mbox{[}dim\mbox{]}} after it is read as input.

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{mpmd_8libmd_8cc_source_l00056}{56}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{mpmd_8libmd_8cc_source}{mpmd.\+libmd.\+cc}}.
